                            <p class="sh4 uppercase mb-[8px] text-blue1">
                    DOWNLOAD
                </p>
            
        <h1 class="h1 text-blue1">
            RStudio Desktop
        </h1>

        
        <div class="mt-[24px]">
            <div class="text-blue1/[.62] body-lg-regular link-p:link-light [&:not(:first-child)]:paragraphs:mt-[24px] break-words">
                Used by millions of people weekly, the RStudio integrated development environment (IDE) is a set of tools built to help you be more productive with R and Python. <br />
<br />
Dont want to download or install anything? Get started with RStudio on <blue-text><a href="https://posit.cloud/plans?utm_source=Website&utm_medium=IDE_Download" target="_blank"><u>Posit Cloud for free</u></a></blue-text>. If you're a professional data scientist looking to download RStudio and also need common enterprise features, don't hesitate to <blue-text><a href="https://posit.co/schedule-a-call/?booking_calendar__c=RStudio_IDE" target="_blank"><u>book a call with us</u></a></blue-text>.<br />
<br />
Want to learn about core or advanced workflows in RStudio? Explore the <blue-text><a href="https://docs.posit.co/ide/user/" target="_blank"><u>RStudio User Guide</u></a></blue-text> or the <blue-text><a href="https://docs.posit.co/ide/user/ide/get-started/" target="_blank"><u>Getting Started</u></a></blue-text> section.
            </div>
        </div>

        <div class="tabs-component col-span-12">

            <div class="tabs flex h-0 overflow-x-scroll">

                
                    <div class="tab mt-[5px] first-of-type:ml-[5px] [&:not(:first-of-type)]:ml-[48px]">
